Play Audio 
Request 
• 
API number: 6000 (0x1770) 
• 
Name: robot_other_speaker_req 
• 
Description: Play audio and specified audio file. 
• 
JSON data area: See table below. 
Field Name 
Type 
Description 
name 
String 
Audio file name to be played (without file extension) 
loop 
Boolean 
Whether to play in a loop (true = loop, false = no loop, if default, not loop) 
Request Example 
5A 01 00 01 00 00 00 20 17 70 00 00 00 00 00 00 
{"name":"collision","loop":true} 
// loop play collision 
7B 22 6E 61 6D 65 22 3A 22 63 6F 6C 6C 69 73 69  
6F 6E 22 2C 22 6C 6F 6F 70 22 3A 74 72 75 65 7D 
Response 
• 
API number: 16000 (0x3E80) 
• 
Name: robot_other_speaker_res 
• 
Description: Response of playing audio 
• 
JSON data area: See table below. 
Field Name 
Type 
Description 
Whether Default 
ret_code 
Number 
API error code 
YES 
create_on 
String 
API upload timestamp 
YES 
err_msg 
String 
Error message 
YES 
Response Example 
{ 
  "ret_code": 0 
} 
5A 01 00 01 00 00 00 0E 3E 80 17 70 00 00 00 00 
7B 22 72 65 74 5F 63 6F 64 65 22 3A 30 7D 
 
Set DO 
This API is used to set the DO (Digital Output) status on the robot controller 
Request 
• 
API number: 6001 (0x1771) 
• 
Name: robot_other_setdo_req 
• 
Description: Set DO 
• 
JSON data area: See table below. 
Field Name 
Type 
Description 
Whether Default 
id 
Number 
id of the DO 
NO 
status 
Boolean 
True is high level, and false is low level. 
NO 
Request Example 
5A 01 00 01 00 00 00 17 17 71 00 00 00 00 00 00 
{"id":3,"status":false} 
// After serialization, the hex is: 
7B 22 69 64 22 3A 33 2C 22 73 74 61 74 75 73 22  
3A 66 61 6C 73 65 7D 
Response 
• 
API number: 16001 (0x3E81) 
• 
Name: robot_other_setdo_res 
• 
Description: Response of set DO 
• 
JSON data area: See table below. 
Field Name 
Type 
Description 
Whether Default 
ret_code 
Number 
API error code 
YES 
create_on 
String 
API upload timestamp 
YES 
err_msg 
String 
Error message 
YES 
Response Example 
Omitted 
 
Batch Set DO 
This API is used to set the DO (Digital Output) status on the robot controller in batches. 
Request 
• 
API number: 6002 (0x1772) 
• 
Name: robot_other_setdos_req 
• 
Description: Batch set DO 
• 
JSON data area: See below. 
// The data area must be a JSON array, each object in the array is the same as in the 6001 instruction 
// The following JSON sets DO 0,1,2,3 at the same time, respectively set to high, high, low, low 
[{"id":0,"status":true},{"id":1,"status":true},{"id":2,"status":false},{"id":3,"status":false}] 
Request Example 
[{"id":0,"status":true},{"id":1,"status":true},{"id":2,"status":false},{"id":3,"status":false},{"id":4,"status":true},{"i
d":5,"status":true},{"id":6,"status":false}] 
Response 
• 
API number: 16002 (0x3E82) 
• 
Name: robot_other_setdos_res 
• 
Description: Response of batch set DO 
• 
JSON data area: See table below. 
Field Name 
Type 
Description 
Whether Default 
ret_code 
Number 
API error code 
YES 
create_on 
String 
API upload timestamp 
YES 
Field Name 
Type 
Description 
Whether Default 
err_msg 
String 
error message 
YES 
Response Example 
Omitted

Set Virtual DI 
This API is used to set the virtual DI (Virtual Digital Iutput) status on the robot controller. 
Request 
• 
API number: 6020 (0x1784) 
• 
Name: robot_other_setvdi_req 
• 
Description: Set virtual DI. 
• 
JSON data area: See table below. 
Field Name 
Type 
Description 
id 
Number 
The id of the virtual DI (the index of the first virtual DI in the DI list is 0, the range of the id is [0, 7]) 
status 
Boolean 
True is high level, and false is low level. 
Request Example 
5A 01 00 01 00 00 00 17 17 84 00 00 00 00 00 00 
{"id":1,"status":false} 
// After serialization, the hex is: 
7B 22 69 64 22 3A 31 2C 22 73 74 61 74 75 73 22  
3A 66 61 6C 73 65 7D

Set Fork Height 
This API is used to set the height of the fork of the forklift. This command will return immediately, so you need to query the 
fork_height_in_place in the 1028 or 1100 command to check whether the fork is in place. 
Request 
• 
API number: 6040 (0x1798) 
• 
Name: robot_other_set_fork_height_req 
• 
Description: Set fork height. 
• 
JSON data area: See table below. 
Field Name 
Type 
Description 
Whether Default 
height 
Number 
Fork height, unit: m 
For pallet track: 1= Rise; 0 = fell 
NO 
Request Example 
5A 01 00 01 00 00 00 0E 17 98 00 00 00 00 00 00 
{"height":1.2} 
// After serialization, the hex is: 
7B 22 68 65 69 67 68 74 22 3A 31 2E 32 7D 
Response 
• 
API number: 16040 (0x3EA8) 
• 
Name: robot_other_set_fork_height_res 
• 
Description: Response of settig fork height 
• 
JSON data area: See table below. 
Field Name 
Type 
Description 
Whether Default 
ret_code 
Number 
API error code 
YES 
Field Name 
Type 
Description 
Whether Default 
create_on 
String 
API upload timestamp 
YES 
err_msg 
String 
Error message 
YES 
Response Example 
{ 
  "ret_code": 0 
} 
5A 01 00 01 00 00 00 0E 3E A8 17 98 00 00 00 00 
7B 22 72 65 74 5F 63 6F 64 65 22 3A 30 7D

Set Fork Forward or Backward 
This API is used to set the fork of the forklift to move forward and backward, and the command will return immediately, so you 
need to query the forward_in_place in the 1028 or 1100 command to check whether the fork is in place. 
Request 
• 
API number: 6042 (0x179A) 
• 
Name: robot_other_set_fork_forward_req 
• 
Description: Set fork forward or backward 
• 
JSON data area: See table below. 
Field 
Name 
Type 
Description 
Whether 
Default 
forward 
Number 
① For the case without cable encoder, 2 = move forward, 1 = move backward, 0 = stop 
② For the case with cable encoder, a positive number indicates the forward distance, while a negative 
number indicates the backward distance, unit m 
NO 
Request Example 
5A 01 00 00 00 00 00 0F 17 9A 00 00 00 00 00 00 
{"forward":1.0} 
// After serialization, the hex is: 
7B 22 66 6F 72 77 61 72 64 22 3A 31 2E 30 7D 
Response 
• 
API number: 16042 (0x3EAA) 
• 
Name: robot_other_set_fork_forward_res 
• 
Description: Response of setting fork forward or backward 
• 
JSON data area: See table below. 
Field Name 
Type 
Description 
Whether Default 
ret_code 
Number 
API error code 
YES 
create_on 
String 
API upload timestamp 
YES 
err_msg 
String 
Error message 
YES 
Response Example 
{

Roller Front Roll 
When rolling, both sides of the baffle are down. 
 
The command will return immediately, so you need to check whether the loading is completed by the roller_state in the 1029 or 
1100 command. Rolling will not fail due to timeout, and the roller will keep rolling until receiving a new command. 
 
Roller motion commands are not accepted during robot movement. 
Request 
• 
API number: 6051 (0x17A3) 
•

Roller Inverse Left and Right 
After using this command to set the inverse , the left and right logic of the roller will be inversed, that is, the left load becomes the 
right load, and the right load becomes the left load. 
Request 
• 
API number: 6068 (0x17B4) 
• 
Name: robot_other_roller_left_right_inverse_req 
• 
Description: Roller inverse left and right 
• 
JSON data area: See table below. 
Field name 
Type 
Description 
inverse 
Boolean 
Whether to inverse , true = inverse , false = not inverse (ie return to normal) 
Request Example 
5A 01 00 01 00 00 00 10 17 B4 00 00 00 00 00 00 
{"inverse":true} 
// inverse left and right 
7B 22 69 6E 76 65 72 73 65 22 3A 74 72 75 65 7D 
Response 
• 
API number: 16068 (0x3EC4) 
• 
Name: robot_other_roller_left_right_inverse_res 
• 
Description: Response of roller inverse left and right 
• 
JSON data area: See table below. 
Field Name 
Type 
Description 
Whether Default 
ret_code 
Number 
API error code 
YES 
create_on 
String 
API upload timestamp 
YES 
err_msg 
String 
Error message 
YES 
Response Example 
{ 
  "ret_code": 0 
} 
5A 01 00 01 00 00 00 0E 3E C4 17 B4 00 00 00 00 
7B 22 72 65 74 5F 63 6F 64 65 22 3A 30 7D 
 
 
Roller Inverse Front and Back 
After using this command to set the inverse, the front and back logic of the roller will be inversed, that is, the front load becomes 
the back load, and the back load becomes the front load.

• 
JSON data area: See table below.

Type 
Description

boolean

{"inverse":true} 
// inverse front and back 
7B 22 69 6E 76 65 72 73 65 22 3A 74 72 75 65 7D

Robot Data Push 
API Error Code 
The API error code is the error code (ret_code) contained in the JSON object in the response data area, using to indicate errors such 
as unsuccessful execution of the request or request error. If ret_code is 0 or default, it means there is no error. If it is not 0, it means 
that an error has occurred. The error codes are shown in the following table: 
Field Name 
Type 
Description 
controller_voltage 
number 
Controller voltage, unit V 
manual_charge 
boolean 
It only indicates whether the robot is connected to the manual charger, but cannot ensure whether the 
power supply is switched on. When the robot is connected to the manual charger, it cannot move (only 
supported by SRC-2000). 
auto_charge 
boolean 
It only indicates whether the robot is connected to the automatic charging pile, but cannot ensure whethe
the power supply is switched on (only supported by SRC-2000). 
electric 
boolean 
True indicates that the relay is on. False indicates that the relay is off. 
ssid 
string 
SSID currently connected to WIFI (The robot needs to support WIFI connection and should have already 
connected, otherwise it is null.) 
rssi 
number 
Signal strength from o to 100 percent currently connected to WIFI (The robot needs to support WIFI 
connection and should have already connected, otherwise it is 0.) 
ap_addr 
string 
MAC address of the AP currently connected 
The error code will only appear in the JSON data in the response data area.

Map Format

Robot Detection 
We use Bonjour for robot detection. 
For more details of Bonjour, please refer to the Apple Developer website https://developer.apple.com/bonjour/. 
After installing Bonjour, you can find the domain of the robot in the LAN by searching for the service type _robokitV2._tcp, and then 
the IP address of the robot can be resolved by domain. 
Example 
Get all services of type _robokitV2._tcp: 
dns-sd -B _robokitV2._tcp 
The list of services is as follows: 
Browsing for _robokitV2._tcp 
Timestamp     A/R Flags if Domain                    Service Type              Instance Name 
16:45:27.577  Add     3 10 local.                    _robokitV2._tcp.            SeerRobot 
Query the domain of a service: 
dns-sd -L SeerRobot _robokitV2._tcp 
The result of domain: 
Lookup SeerRobot._robokitV2._tcp.local 
16:46:45.624  SeerRobot._robokitV2._tcp.local. can be reached at seer-yys-win.local.:19204 (interface 10) Flags: 1 
Get IP address based on domain: 
dns-sd -G v4 seer-yys-win.local 
The result of IP address: 
Timestamp     A/R Flags if Hostname                  Address                                      TTL 
16:47:49.544  Add     2  8 seer-yys-win.local.       192.168.4.129                                120 
The result is 192.168.4.129.
